            options: {},
        }

        const countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {"countries":["ES","HU","IN","MX","PH","SG","TH","TR"]};

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":[]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

	crypto.randomUUID = () =>
		([1e7] + -1e3 + -4e3 + -8e3 + -1e11).replace(/[018]/g, (c) =>
			(c ^ (crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(1))[0] & (15 >> (c / 4)))).toString(16),
		);
}</script>

	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"rTmH3s1D","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="rarity">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font"><a href="/wiki/Rarity" title="Rarity">Rarity</a></h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Common</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="renewable">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font"><a href="/wiki/Renewable_resource" title="Renewable resource">Renewable</a></h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><b>Uncraftable, Luck&#8204;<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">JE</a>  only</span></i>&#93;</sup>, Decay&#8204;<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><span title="This statement only applies to Bedrock Edition"><a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition">BE</a>  only</span></i>&#93;</sup></b>: No<br /><b>All others</b>: Yes</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="stackable">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Stackable</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">BE: No<br />JE: No&#8204;<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><span title="This statement does not apply to upcoming versions of Minecraft">until</span> <a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_Combat_Tests" title="Java Edition Combat Tests">JE Combat Tests</a></i>&#93;</sup><br />Yes (16)&#8204;<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><span title="This statement applies only to upcoming versions of Minecraft.">upcoming:</span> <a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_Combat_Tests" title="Java Edition Combat Tests">JE Combat Tests</a></i>&#93;</sup></div>
</div>
</aside>

<b>Potions</b> are bottled substances designed to inflict <a href="/wiki/Effects" class="mw-redirect" title="Effects">effects</a>. They are created by <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewing</a> and when drunk give the player an <a href="/wiki/Effect" title="Effect">effect</a> for a limited time. All potions are brewed from a <b>water bottle</b>, which is considered a type of potion but has no effects.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Obtaining">Obtaining</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mob_loot">Mob loot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Witches">Witches</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Witch" title="Witch">Witches</a> can drop potions of Healing, Fire Resistance, Swiftness, or Water Breathing if they die while drinking that potion.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wandering_traders">Wandering traders</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Wandering_trader" class="mw-redirect" title="Wandering trader">Wandering traders</a> have a chance to drop a Potion of Invisibility if they die while drinking the potion.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fishing">Fishing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Water_bottle" class="mw-redirect" title="Water bottle">Water bottles</a> can be <a href="/wiki/Fishing" title="Fishing">fished</a> up as junk items.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Brewing">Brewing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" style="font-style: italic; margin-left: 1em;">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">Brewing</a></div>
<p>Almost all potions are obtained by <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewing</a>.
</p><p>The Potion of Luck&#8204;<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">JE</a>  only</span></i>&#93;</sup> and the Potion of Decay&#8204;<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><span title="This statement only applies to Bedrock Edition"><a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition">BE</a>  only</span></i>&#93;</sup> cannot be brewed. A command to give a Luck Potion is <code>/<a href="/wiki/Commands/give" title="Commands/give">give</a> @s minecraft:potion{Potion:luck}</code>, while a Potion of Decay can be obtained via <code>/<a href="/wiki/Commands/give" title="Commands/give">give</a> @s potion 1 36</code>. Both are also available in the <a href="/wiki/Creative_inventory" class="mw-redirect" title="Creative inventory">creative inventory</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chest_loot">Chest loot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Two Health II potions can be found in the brewing stand on ships in <a href="/wiki/End_cities" class="mw-redirect" title="End cities">end cities</a>, and one splash potion of Weakness can be found in a brewing stand in <a href="/wiki/Igloo" title="Igloo">igloo</a> basements.
</p><p>in <a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock Edition</i></a>, the cauldron in a <a href="/wiki/Swamp_hut" title="Swamp hut">swamp hut</a> contains a random potion.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bartering">Bartering</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Piglin" title="Piglin">Piglins</a> may <a href="/wiki/Barter" class="mw-redirect" title="Barter">barter</a> a potion or a splash potion of Fire Resistance when given a <a href="/wiki/Gold_ingot" class="mw-redirect" title="Gold ingot">gold ingot</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage">Usage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Potions are used by pressing and holding <span class="explain" title="Defaults to right click on mouse or left trigger on most controllers.">use</span> with the potion bottle in hand, as with all consumable items. When drunk they bestow the corresponding <a href="/wiki/Status_effect" class="mw-redirect" title="Status effect">status effect</a> to the player.
</p><p>Drinking a potion while already under the effects of the same potion does not add onto the effect's duration, but simply resets it. A potion effect does not "downgrade" if a lower level is activated. For example, if a <a href="/wiki/Player" title="Player">player</a> has <a href="/wiki/Regeneration" title="Regeneration">Regeneration</a> II, drinking a regular potion of Regeneration does not have any effect.
</p><p>Using a potion on a cauldron does not transfer the potion to the cauldron, but begins to play the drinking animation.&#8204;<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><span title="This statement only applies to Java Edition"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">JE</a>  only</span></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Modifiers">Modifiers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" style="font-style: italic; margin-left: 1em;">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">Brewing</a></div>
<p>Potions can be modified in five ways. 
</p>
<ol><li>Brewing <a href="/wiki/Glowstone_dust" class="mw-redirect" title="Glowstone dust">glowstone dust</a> into certain potions will <i>enhance</i> their level of effect.</li>
<li>Adding <a href="/wiki/Redstone" class="mw-redirect" title="Redstone">redstone</a> will <i>extend</i> the duration of the effect.</li>
<li>Brewing <a href="/wiki/Gunpowder" title="Gunpowder">gunpowder</a> into a potion makes it into a <i>splash</i> potion (area effect).</li>
<li>Adding <a href="/wiki/Dragon%27s_breath" class="mw-redirect" title="Dragon&#39;s breath">dragon's breath</a> to a splash potion creates a <a href="/wiki/Lingering_potion" class="mw-redirect" title="Lingering potion">lingering potion</a> (area effect that lingers on the ground).</li>
<li>Brewing a <a href="/wiki/Fermented_spider_eye" class="mw-redirect" title="Fermented spider eye">fermented spider eye</a> into specific potions modifies their effect, usually inverting it, which is referred to as "corruption".</li></ol>
<p>The modifications of Enhancement and Extension are mutually exclusive. 
</p><p>Enhancing most potions trades some of its duration for a bigger effect. For example, the base Regeneration works for 44 seconds whereas Regeneration II lasts for only 22 seconds but heals more per tick during that time. 
</p><p>Extending a potion generally makes it last <sup>8</sup>&#8260;<sub>3</sub> as long as its base potion, so a duration of 3 minutes becomes 8 minutes. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Corruption">Corruption</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The usual result of corruption is to invert the potion's effect (for example Swiftness becomes Slowness). Interestingly, corrupting Poison (continuous damage effect) creates a Potion of Harming, an instant damage effect, instead of the continuous healing effect (regeneration) one would normally expect. Corrupting a Potion of Night Vision turns it into a Potion of Invisibility rather than an inverse effect that might be something like blindness.
</p><p>Corrupting an extended or enhanced potion results in a corrupted potion with the same modifier, if it is supported by the corrupted effect. All of the "corrupted" potions except Harming can be extended, but it is the only one that can be enhanced. In <a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock Edition</i></a>, the corruption of Healing II or Poison II potions results in a potion of Harming I.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Base_potions">Base potions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Base potions are potions that have no effect when the player drinks them, but are necessary as the basis for other potions.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Uncraftable_Potion">Uncraftable Potion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition"><i>Java Edition</i></a>, the Uncraftable Potion is a potion with no effect that is unobtainable in regular gameplay.
</p><p>It is also available in splash potion and lingering potion forms, as well as for tipped arrows.
</p><p>It can be obtained using the following command: <code>/<a href="/wiki/Commands/give" title="Commands/give">give</a> @s minecraft:potion{Potion:"minecraft:empty"}</code>. It is also obtained any time a potion has invalid or missing potion effect tags, and thus serves as a placeholder.
</p>
<table class="wikitable" style="text-align: center;" data-description="Unused potions">

</td>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Java_Edition_23w13a_or_b"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_23w13a_or_b" title="Java Edition 23w13a or b">Java Edition 23w13a_or_b</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="msgbox msgbox-mini msgbox-orange" style="max-width: 50em;">
<div id="msgbox-icon"> <div id="msgbox-iconimage" style=""> <span class="sprite comment-sprite" style="background-position:-16px -32px"></span></div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Undead_mobs">Undead mobs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The effects given by Potions of Healing and Harming are opposite on undead mobs, which includes skeletons and zombies. Potions of Healing cause harm, and Harming heals them. In addition, undead mobs are not affected by Poison or Regeneration. 
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock Edition</i></a>, hitting an undead mob with a Regeneration Potion will always register as Regeneration I, no matter the level of the used potion.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mud_conversion">Mud conversion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Using a water bottle, splash water bottle, or lingering water bottle on <a href="/wiki/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coarse_dirt" class="mw-redirect" title="Coarse dirt">coarse dirt</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Rooted_dirt" class="mw-redirect" title="Rooted dirt">rooted dirt</a> will convert it into <a href="/wiki/Mud" title="Mud">mud</a>, returning a glass bottle with it. This process can be automated with a <a href="/wiki/Dispenser" title="Dispenser">dispenser</a>. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Filling_cauldrons_with_Potions">Filling cauldrons with Potions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition"><i>Bedrock</i></a> and <a href="/wiki/Legacy_Console_Edition" title="Legacy Console Edition">Legacy Console</a> editions potion bottles may be used on a cauldron to fill it. Using a glass bottle on a cauldron filled with a potion drains it and fills the bottle. Potions cannot be combined in a cauldron, nor can they be mixed with water, but as an added bonus if you use a stack of arrows in a full cauldron you get a stack of tipped arrows. for 1 layer you get 16, 2 layers 32.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Custom_effects">Custom effects</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition"><i>Java Edition</i></a>, potions can also be obtained with any status effect using <code>/<a href="/wiki/Commands/give" title="Commands/give">give</a></code> and the tag <code>custom_potion_effects</code>, which is an array of effects for the potion. See <a href="/wiki/Item_format#Potion_Effects" class="mw-redirect" title="Item format">Item format#Potion Effects</a> for more information, and <a href="/wiki/Status_effect" class="mw-redirect" title="Status effect">status effect</a> for a list of effects and IDs.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Data_values">Data values</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="ID">ID</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Item_data">Item data</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Java_Edition">Java Edition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="treeview">
<ul><li><span title="TAG_Compound"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-48px -16px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;tag</span>: The item's <b>tag</b> tag.</li></ul>
<ul><li><ul><li><span title="TAG_List"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-32px -32px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;custom_potion_effects</span>: The custom <a href="/wiki/Potion_effects" class="mw-redirect" title="Potion effects">potion effects</a> (status effects) this potion or tipped arrow has.
<ul><li><span title="TAG_Compound"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-48px -16px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span> One of these for each effect.
<ul><li><span title="TAG_String"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-32px -16px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;id</span>: The <a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_data_values#Effects" title="Java Edition data values">resource location of the effect</a>.</li>
<li><span title="TAG_Byte"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-0px -0px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;amplifier</span>: The amplifier of the effect, with level I having value 0.  Negative levels are discussed <a href="/wiki/Status_effect#negativelevels" class="mw-redirect" title="Status effect">here</a>. Optional, and defaults to level I.</li>
<li><span title="TAG_Int"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-48px -0px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;duration</span>: The duration of the effect in <a href="/wiki/Tick" title="Tick">ticks</a>.  Values 0 or lower are treated as 1.  Optional, and defaults to 1 tick.</li>
<li><span title="TAG_Byte"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-0px -0px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;ambient</span>: 1 or 0 (true/false) - whether or not this is an effect provided by a beacon and therefore should be less intrusive on the screen. Optional, and defaults to false.</li>
<li><span title="TAG_Byte"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-0px -0px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;show_particles</span>: 1 or 0 (true/false) - whether or not this effect produces particles. Optional, and defaults to true.</li>
<li><span title="TAG_Byte"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-0px -0px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;show_icon</span>: 1 or 0 (true/false) - true if effect icon is shown. false if no icon is shown.</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><span title="TAG_String"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-32px -16px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;Potion</span>: The <a href="/wiki/Potion#Item_data" title="Potion">name of the default potion effect</a>. This name differs from the <a href="/wiki/Status_effect" class="mw-redirect" title="Status effect">status effect</a> name. For example, the value for an "Instant Health II" potion is "minecraft:strong_healing".  A potion or tipped arrow getting its effects from this tag is named with the proper effect. The default value is "minecraft:empty", which gives it the "Uncraftable" name.</li>
<li><span title="TAG_Int"><span class="sprite nbt-sprite" style="background-position:-48px -0px;background-size:64px auto;height:16px;width:16px"></span></span><span class="nowrap" style="font-weight: bold;">&#160;CustomPotionColor</span>: The item uses this custom color, and area-of-effect clouds, arrows, and splash and lingering potions use it for their particle effects. This color does not extend, however, to the particles given off by entities who ultimately receive the effect. The numeric color codes are equal to the hex code of the color converted to a decimal number, or can alternatively be calculated from the Red, Green and Blue components using this formula: <b><span style="color:red">Red</span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Logical_shift" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Logical shift">&lt;&lt;</a>16 + <span style="color:green">Green</span>&lt;&lt;8 + <span style="color:blue">Blue</span></b>. For positive values larger than 0x00FFFFFF, the top byte is ignored. All negative values produce white.</li></ul></li></ul>
</div>

The source of the effects is irrelevant for the purposes of this advancement. Other status effects may be applied to the player, but are ignored for this advancement.<br /><i>This is a hidden advancement, meaning that it can be viewed by the player only after completing it, regardless of if its child advancement(s), if any, have been completed.</i></td><td><code>nether/all_effects

<table class="wikitable" data-description="History" style="image-rendering: pixelated;"><tbody><tr><th colspan="6"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_Beta" title="Java Edition Beta">Java Edition Beta</a></th></tr>
<tr><th rowspan="1" colspan="5"><a target="_self" rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/0/http://notch.tumblr.com/post/779956568/the-rationale-for-redstone">July 7, 2010</a></th><td><a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">Alchemy</a> was first hinted by <a href="/wiki/Notch" class="mw-redirect" title="Notch">Notch</a> when he explained why <a href="/wiki/Redstone_ore" class="mw-redirect" title="Redstone ore">redstone ore</a> disintegrates into "<a href="/wiki/Redstone" class="mw-redirect" title="Redstone">dust</a>". He states that dust would be used later in potions.</td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="6"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_version_history" title="Java Edition version history"><i>Java Edition</i></a></th></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="5" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.0.0" title="Java Edition 1.0.0">1.0.0</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="4">Beta 1.9 Prerelease 2</th><td><a href="/wiki/Jeb" class="mw-redirect" title="Jeb">Jeb</a> tweeted a screenshot showing potion durations and <a href="/wiki/Glass_bottle" class="mw-redirect" title="Glass bottle">glass bottles</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</td></tr><tr><td>Potions are <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewed</a> using <a href="/wiki/Cauldron" title="Cauldron">cauldrons</a><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> by combining ingredients and other potions in cauldrons. Cauldrons, although they are functional and can be used to brew potions, are unavailable in this update.</td></tr><tr><td>In total, there are 161 possible potion combinations and 2,653 different types of potions.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></td></tr><tr><td><a href="/wiki/Jeb" class="mw-redirect" title="Jeb">Jeb</a> later tweeted that both <a href="/wiki/Notch" class="mw-redirect" title="Notch">Notch</a> and he had come up with a different way to <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brew</a> potions, which was revealed to be <a href="/wiki/Brewing_stand" class="mw-redirect" title="Brewing stand">brewing stands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">Beta 1.9 Prerelease 3</th><td><a href="/wiki/Brewing_stand" class="mw-redirect" title="Brewing stand">Brewing stands</a> have been implemented, which has replaced the (previously unimplemented) <a href="/wiki/Cauldron" title="Cauldron">cauldrons</a>' <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewing</a> functionality, so potions are now obtainable without mods. Potions Brewed in the previous version will now be glitched. Water Bottles have been added.</td></tr>

<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="2">12w34a</th><td><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/minecraft_gamepedia/images/9/99/Potion_of_Invisibility_JE1_BE1.png/revision/latest?cb=20191027042045" class="image"><img alt="Potion of Invisibility JE1 BE1" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="Potion of Invisibility JE1 BE1.png" data-image-key="Potion_of_Invisibility_JE1_BE1.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/minecraft_gamepedia/images/9/99/Potion_of_Invisibility_JE1_BE1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20191027042045" class="lazyload" /></a> Added potions of <a href="/wiki/Invisibility" title="Invisibility">Invisibility</a>.
</td></tr><tr><td>Potions of Night Vision are now <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewable</a>.</td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">12w38a</th><td><a href="/wiki/Witch" title="Witch">Witches</a> now cast potions at <a href="/wiki/Player" title="Player">players</a> and can rarely <a href="/wiki/Drops" title="Drops">drop</a> potions upon <a href="/wiki/Death" class="mw-redirect" title="Death">death</a>.</td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">12w39a</th><td>Potions are now customizable using NBT editors or MCEdit.</td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="2" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.6.1" title="Java Edition 1.6.1">1.6.1</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="1"><a href="/wiki/Category:Unknown_version_history" title="Category:Unknown version history">?</a></th><td>Potions of <a href="/wiki/Weakness" title="Weakness">Weakness</a> now reduce <a href="/wiki/Damage" title="Damage">damage</a> by half hearts, instead of 1 heart as it was before.</td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">13w23a</th><td>Potions of <a href="/wiki/Healing" title="Healing">Healing</a> and <a href="/wiki/Regeneration" title="Regeneration">Regeneration</a> have been nerfed (by 33.3% and 50%).</td></tr> 
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="2" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.7.2" title="Java Edition 1.7.2">1.7.2</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="2">13w36a</th><td><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/minecraft_gamepedia/images/1/13/Potion_of_Water_Breathing_JE1_BE1.png/revision/latest?cb=20191027042519" class="image"><img alt="Potion of Water Breathing JE1 BE1" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="Potion of Water Breathing JE1 BE1.png" data-image-key="Potion_of_Water_Breathing_JE1_BE1.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/minecraft_gamepedia/images/1/13/Potion_of_Water_Breathing_JE1_BE1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20191027042519" class="lazyload" /></a> Added potions of <a href="/wiki/Water_Breathing" title="Water Breathing">Water Breathing</a>.

<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="1" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.8.1" title="Java Edition 1.8.1">1.8.1</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">pre1</th><td>Potion of Leaping can now be extended.</td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="10" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.9" title="Java Edition 1.9">1.9</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="4">15w31a</th><td>Numeric IDs are no longer used for potions. Instead, an NBT "Potion" <a href="/wiki/Tag" title="Tag">tag</a> is used, e.g. <code>/<a href="/wiki/Commands/give" title="Commands/give">give</a> @p minecraft:potion 1 0 {Potion:"minecraft:swiftness"}</code>. See <a href="/wiki/Potion/Before_1.9" title="Potion/Before 1.9">here</a> for the old numeric IDs. This means the order of potion effects have changed in the Creative inventory.

<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="4">15w33a</th><td>Added <a href="/wiki/Lingering_potion" class="mw-redirect" title="Lingering potion">lingering potions</a>, which are <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewed</a> with <a href="/wiki/Splash_potion" class="mw-redirect" title="Splash potion">splash potions</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dragon_breath" class="mw-redirect" title="Dragon breath">dragon breath</a> after splash potions are brewed with potions and <a href="/wiki/Gunpowder" title="Gunpowder">gunpowder</a>.
</td></tr><tr><td>The duration of potions of <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">Poison</a> has been extended, the duration of potions of <a href="/wiki/Regeneration" title="Regeneration">Regeneration</a> has been extended, and the duration of potions of <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">Poison</a> II has been reduced.</td></tr><tr><td>Potion of <a href="/wiki/Strength" title="Strength">Strength</a> has been changed from 130% increase to 3-point increase.</td></tr><tr><td>Potion of <a href="/wiki/Weakness" title="Weakness">Weakness</a> has been changed to 4-point decrease, was 0.5-point decrease.</td></tr>

<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="3">16w38a</th><td>The uncraftable potion is now magenta, has no glint, and is now obtained anytime a potion is specified with invalid or missing potion effect <a href="/wiki/Tag" title="Tag">tags</a>.
</td></tr><tr><td>Due to the <a href="/wiki/Water_bottle" class="mw-redirect" title="Water bottle">water bottle</a> without tags being changed to the uncraftable potion, the <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewing</a> icon has also been changed to the uncraftable potion in <a href="/wiki/Creative" title="Creative">creative</a> <a href="/wiki/Inventory" title="Inventory">inventory</a>.</td></tr><tr><td>The uncraftable potion has been removed from the <a href="/wiki/Creative" title="Creative">creative</a> <a href="/wiki/Inventory" title="Inventory">inventory</a>.</td></tr>

<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="2" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.16.2" title="Java Edition 1.16.2">1.16.2</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="2">20w28a</th><td>Water bottles can now be obtained through <a href="/wiki/Bartering" title="Bartering">bartering</a>.</td></tr><tr><td>Potions and splash potions of Fire Resistance now have a <sup>8</sup>&#8260;<sub>459</sub> (~1.74%) chance of being offered by <a href="/wiki/Piglin" title="Piglin">piglins</a> when bartering.</td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="1" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.18" title="Java Edition 1.18">1.18</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">21w39a</th><td>Potions of Water Breathing can now generate in <a href="/wiki/Buried_treasure" class="mw-redirect" title="Buried treasure">buried treasure</a> chests.</td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="4" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.19" title="Java Edition 1.19">1.19</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">Deep Dark Experimental Snapshot 1</th><td>Potions of Healing now generate in <a href="/wiki/Ancient_city" class="mw-redirect" title="Ancient city">ancient city</a> chests.</td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">22w11a</th><td>Water bottles can now be used on <a href="/wiki/Dirt" title="Dirt">dirt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coarse_dirt" class="mw-redirect" title="Coarse dirt">coarse dirt</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Rooted_dirt" class="mw-redirect" title="Rooted dirt">rooted dirt</a> to turn it into <a href="/wiki/Mud" title="Mud">mud</a>.</td></tr>
<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="2">22w13a</th><td>Potions of Healing no longer generate in <a href="/wiki/Ancient_city" class="mw-redirect" title="Ancient city">ancient city</a> <a href="/wiki/Chest" title="Chest">chests</a>.</td></tr><tr><td>Potions of Regeneration may now be found in <a href="/wiki/Ancient_city" class="mw-redirect" title="Ancient city">ancient city</a> <a href="/wiki/Chest" title="Chest">chests</a>.</td></tr>

<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="2" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.20" title="Java Edition 1.20">1.20</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="2">23w12a</th><td>Wither <a href="/wiki/Effect" title="Effect">effect</a> particle colors have been adjusted to make them more distinguishable.
</td></tr><tr><td>The potion of <a href="/wiki/Slow_Falling" title="Slow Falling">Slow Falling</a> has had its color tweaked to make it more distinguishable from the potion of <a href="/wiki/Invisibility" title="Invisibility">Invisibility</a>.</td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="2" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Java_Edition_1.20.2" title="Java Edition 1.20.2">1.20.2</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="2">23w32a</th><td>Game no longer uses numerical values for potion IDs.</td></tr><tr><td>Renamed the following tags:
<ul><li><code>CustomPotionEffects</code> -&gt; <code>custom_potion_effects</code></li>
<li><code>Id</code> (integer) -&gt; <code>id</code> (string, resource location)</li>
<li><code>Ambient</code> -&gt; <code>ambient</code></li>
<li><code>Amplifier</code> -&gt; <code>amplifier</code></li>
<li><code>Duration</code> -&gt; <code>duration</code></li>
<li><code>ShowParticles</code> -&gt; <code>show_particles</code></li>
<li><code>ShowIcon</code> -&gt; <code>show_icon</code></li></ul></td></tr>

<tr><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">Combat Test 8b</th><td>Potions (and liquid food) can now be drank faster (20 ticks, was 32 ticks).</td></tr>

<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="1" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Pocket_Edition_v0.13.0_alpha" title="Pocket Edition v0.13.0 alpha">v0.13.0</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">build 1</th><td>Potions of <a href="/wiki/Leaping" class="mw-redirect" title="Leaping">Leaping</a> are now obtainable in <a href="/wiki/Survival" title="Survival">survival</a>.</td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="4" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Pocket_Edition_v0.14.0_alpha" title="Pocket Edition v0.14.0 alpha">v0.14.0</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="4">build 1</th><td>Potions can now be used to fill 1/3 layer of <a href="/wiki/Cauldron" title="Cauldron">cauldron</a>, filling cauldron with different <a href="/wiki/Liquids" class="mw-redirect" title="Liquids">liquid</a> empties the cauldron.
</td></tr><tr><td>Using a <a href="/wiki/Glass_bottle" class="mw-redirect" title="Glass bottle">glass bottle</a> to a <a href="/wiki/Cauldron" title="Cauldron">cauldron</a> filled by a potion now fills the glass bottle with that potion.</td></tr><tr><td><a href="/wiki/Swamp_hut" title="Swamp hut">Swamp huts</a> now generate <a href="/wiki/Cauldron" title="Cauldron">cauldrons</a> filled with a random potion, making potions now obtainable in <a href="/wiki/Survival" title="Survival">survival</a> without <a href="/wiki/Brewing" title="Brewing">brewing</a>.</td></tr><tr><td>Potions of <a href="/wiki/Healing" title="Healing">Healing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fire_Resistance" title="Fire Resistance">Fire Resistance</a>, <a href="/wiki/Water_Breathing" title="Water Breathing">Water Breathing</a> and <a href="/wiki/Swiftness" class="mw-redirect" title="Swiftness">Swiftness</a> can now be obtained by killing <a href="/wiki/Witch" title="Witch">witches</a> while they're drinking potions.</td></tr>
<tr><th class="nowrap" rowspan="1" colspan="2"><a href="/wiki/Pocket_Edition_v0.16.0_alpha" title="Pocket Edition v0.16.0 alpha">v0.16.0</a></th><th colspan="3" rowspan="1">build 4</th><td><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/minecraft_gamepedia/images/2/2c/Potion_of_Decay_BE1.png/revision/latest?cb=20191027042005" class="image"><img alt="Potion of Decay BE1" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="32" data-image-name="Potion of Decay BE1.png" data-image-key="Potion_of_Decay_BE1.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/minecraft_gamepedia/images/2/2c/Potion_of_Decay_BE1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/32?cb=20191027042005" class="lazyload" /></a> Added potions of <a href="/wiki/Wither_(status_effect)" class="mw-redirect" title="Wither (status effect)">Decay</a>.</td></tr>

</td></tr><tr><td>Removed enchantment glint from splash potions.</td></tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Issues">Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Issues relating to "Potion" are maintained on the <a href="/wiki/Bug_tracker" title="Bug tracker">bug tracker</a>. Report issues <a target="_self" rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://bugs.mojang.com/issues/?jql=project%20in%20%28MC%2C%20MCPE%29%20and%20%28resolution%20is%20empty%20or%20resolution%20in%20%281%2C%202%2C%206%29%29%20and%20%28summary%20~%20%22Potion%22%29%20order%20by%20resolution%20desc">there</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>A potion can reach a maximum tier of 127, but using the <code>/<a href="/wiki/Commands/effect" title="Commands/effect">effect</a></code> <a href="/wiki/Commands" title="Commands">command</a>, effect levels can reach 255.</li>
<li>When a player drinks two potions by quickly switching to another potion immediately after drinking one, the second drinking animation is not shown.<sup class="noprint nowrap Inline-Template" title="">&#91;<i><a target="_self" class="text" href="https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Talk:Potion"><span title="Still in recent versions?" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted">verify</span></a></i>&#93;</sup></li>
<li>A potion of <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">Poison</a> II lasts for 22.5 seconds, but it is displayed as 22 seconds because the <a href="/wiki/Item" title="Item">item</a> hover display shows rounded-down integer values.</li>
<li>The "Local Brewery" <a href="/wiki/Advancement" title="Advancement">advancement</a> uses the Uncraftable Potion texture for its icon.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Unused_potions">Unused potions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fminecraft.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FPotion%3Faction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition" title="Bedrock Edition">Bedrock Edition</a></i> has <a href="/wiki/History_of_textures/Unused_textures#Unused_potions" title="History of textures/Unused textures">unused potion textures</a> for several <a href="/wiki/Effect" title="Effect">effects</a>, along with their <a href="/wiki/Splash_Potion#Unused_splash_potions" title="Splash Potion">splash variants</a>. These effects are: <a href="/wiki/Absorption" title="Absorption">Absorption</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blindness" title="Blindness">Blindness</a>, <a href="/wiki/Haste" title="Haste">Haste</a>, <a href="/wiki/Health_Boost" title="Health Boost">Health Boost</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hunger" title="Hunger">Hunger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mining_Fatigue" title="Mining Fatigue">Mining Fatigue</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nausea" title="Nausea">Nausea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Resistance" title="Resistance">Resistance</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saturation" title="Saturation">Saturation</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Levitation" title="Levitation">Levitation</a>, as well as the <a href="/wiki/Luck" title="Luck">Luck</a> potion textures also present in <a href="/wiki/Java_Edition" title="Java Edition">Java Edition</a>. These unused textures were added along with the other potion textures in <a href="/wiki/Pocket_Edition_v0.12.1_alpha" title="Pocket Edition v0.12.1 alpha">Pocket Edition v0.12.1 alpha</a>, except for the potion of levitation, which was added in <a href="/wiki/Pocket_Edition_1.0.0" title="Pocket Edition 1.0.0">Pocket Edition 1.0.0</a>. The textures were changed along with the other potion textures during the <a href="/wiki/Texture_update" class="mw-redirect" title="Texture update">texture update</a> in <a href="/wiki/Bedrock_Edition_1.10.0" title="Bedrock Edition 1.10.0">Bedrock Edition 1.10.0</a>. Strangely, the potion of levitation texture is a duplicate of the splash potion of levitation texture.
</p>
